# Kolory

GREEN='\033[0;32m'
YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
NC='\033[0m' # No Color

# 1. BACKUP
echo "ğŸ“¦ KROK 1/5: Tworzenie backupu..."
BACKUP_DIR="backups/pre-cleanup-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)"

FILES_TO_DELETE=(
    # Legacy PHP
    "api-add-comment.php"
    "api-add-comment-optimized.php"
    "api-get-comments.php"
    "api-get-comments-optimized.php"
    "api-csrf-token.php"
    "api-csrf-token-optimized.php"
    "config-enhanced.php"
    "config-optimized.php"
    "db_config.php"
    
    # Legacy JS

    "app-optimized.js"

    "images/photo3.jpg"
    "images/photo4.jpg"
    "images/studio/studio1.png"
    "images/studio/studio2.png"
    "images/studio/studio3.png"
    "images/studio/studio4.png"
    "public/images/favicon.jpg"
)

# Backup plikÃ³w

for file in "${FILES_TO_DELETE[@]}"; do
    if [ -f "$file" ]; then
        mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR/$(dirname "$file")"
        cp "$file" "$BACKUP_DIR/$file"
        echo "  âœ“ $file"
    fi
done

# 2. USUWANIE
echo "ğŸ—‘ï¸  KROK 2/5: Usuwanie nieuÅ¼ywanych plikÃ³w..."
DELETED_COUNT=0
DELETED_SIZE=0

for file in "${FILES_TO_DELETE[@]}"; do
    if [ -f "$file" ]; then
        SIZE=$(stat -f%z "$file" 2>/dev/null || stat -c%s "$file" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
        rm "$file"
        DELETED_COUNT=$((DELETED_COUNT + 1))
        DELETED_SIZE=$((DELETED_SIZE + SIZE))
        echo "  âœ“ UsuniÄ™to: $file"
    fi
done

echo -e "${GREEN}âœ“ UsuniÄ™to: $DELETED_COUNT plikÃ³w (~$((DELETED_SIZE / 1024)) KB)${NC}"
echo ""

# 3. UPORZÄ„DKOWANIE DOKUMENTACJI

        echo "  âœ“ Przeniesiono: $doc â†’ docs/archive/"
    fi
done

echo -e "${GREEN}âœ“ Dokumentacja uporzÄ…dkowana${NC}"

# 4. WERYFIKACJA

    echo -e "  ${GREEN}âœ“ GÅ‚Ã³wne katalogi OK${NC}"
else
    echo -e "  ${RED}âœ— BÅÄ„D: Brak kluczowych katalogÃ³w!${NC}"
    exit 1
fi

# 5. PODSUMOWANIE
echo "ğŸ“Š KROK 5/5: Podsumowanie"
echo "================================"
echo -e "UsuniÄ™to plikÃ³w: ${GREEN}$DELETED_COUNT${NC}"
echo -e "Zwolniono miejsca: ${GREEN}~$((DELETED_SIZE / 1024)) KB${NC}"
echo -e "Backup: ${YELLOW}$BACKUP_DIR${NC}"
echo ""
echo -e "${GREEN}âœ“ CZYSZCZENIE ZAKOÅƒCZONE SUKCESEM!${NC}"
echo ""
echo "ğŸ“‹ NASTÄ˜PNE KROKI:"
echo "1. Uruchom: pnpm dev (sprawdÅº czy strona dziaÅ‚a)"
echo "2. Uruchom: pnpm test (sprawdÅº testy)"
echo "3. Uruchom: pnpm build (zbuduj produkcyjnÄ… wersjÄ™)"
echo "4. JeÅ›li wszystko OK: git add . && git commit && git push"

echo "âš ï¸  W razie problemÃ³w:"
echo "   PrzywrÃ³Ä‡ backup: cp -r $BACKUP_DIR/* ./"
echo ""
Jak uÅ¼yÄ‡:

ğŸ“¦ CZÄ˜ÅšÄ† 3: KOMPONENTY REACT
Ze wzglÄ™du na dÅ‚ugoÅ›Ä‡, podzielÄ™ to na osobne pliki. Oto pierwszy, najwaÅ¼niejszy:

Plik: src/features/polana-klamstw/components/ChapterReader.tsx
tsx
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Chapter } from '../types';
import Navigation from './Navigation';
import '../styles/reader.css';

interface ChapterReaderProps {
  chapterId: string;
}

const ChapterReader: React.FC<ChapterReaderProps> = ({ chapterId }) => {
  const [chapter, setChapter] = useState<Chapter | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const loadChapter = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      
      try {
        const response = await fetch(`/data/polana-klamstw/${chapterId}.json`);
        
        if (!response.ok) {
          throw new Error('RozdziaÅ‚ nie zostaÅ‚ znaleziony');
        }
        
        const data: Chapter = await response.json();
        setChapter(data);
      } catch (err) {
        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Nieznany bÅ‚Ä…d');
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    loadChapter();
  }, [chapterId]);

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="chapter-reader loading">
        <div className="spinner" />
        <p>Åadowanie rozdziaÅ‚u...</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (error || !chapter) {
    return (
      <div className="chapter-reader error">
        <h2>BÅ‚Ä…d</h2>
        <p>{error || 'Nie udaÅ‚o siÄ™ zaÅ‚adowaÄ‡ rozdziaÅ‚u'}</p>
        <a href="/polana-klamstw" className="button">
          WrÃ³Ä‡ do spisu treÅ›ci
        </a>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <article className="chapter-reader">
      <header className="chapter-header">
        <p className="chapter-part">{chapter.partName}</p>
        <h1 className="chapter-title">{chapter.title}</h1>
      </header>

      <div 
        className="chapter-content"
        dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: formatContent(chapter.content) }}
      />

      <Navigation
        prevChapter={chapter.prevChapter}
        nextChapter={chapter.nextChapter}
      />
    </article>
  );
};

// Formatowanie treÅ›ci (Markdown-like -> HTML)
function formatContent(content: string): string {
  return content
    // NagÅ‚Ã³wki
    .replace(/^### (.+)$/gm, '<h3>$1</h3>')
    .replace(/^## (.+)$/gm, '<h2>$1</h2>')
    .replace(/^# (.+)$/gm, '<h1>$1</h1>')
    
    // Pogrubienie i kursywa
    .replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
    .replace(/\*(.+?)\*/g, '<em>$1</em>')
    
    // Listy
    .replace(/^\* (.+)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
    .replace(/(<li>.*<\/li>)/s, '<ul>$1</ul>')
    
    // Akapity
    .split('\n\n')
    .map(para => para.trim() ? `<p>${para}</p>` : '')
    .join('\n');
}

export default ChapterReader;

ğŸš€ SZYBKI SKRYPT - AUTOMATYCZNE KOPIOWANIE

3. Mixer (kontroler efektÃ³w)
Plik: src/features/dj-barbara/components/Mixer.tsx

tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';

const Mixer: React.FC = () => {
  const [echo, setEcho] = useState(90);
  const [truth, setTruth] = useState(10);
  const [manipulation, setManipulation] = useState(100);

  return (
    <div className="dj-mixer">
      <h3>ğŸ›ï¸ Mixer Controls</h3>
      
      <div className="mixer-control">
        <label>Echo Level</label>
        <input 
          type="range" 
          min="0" 
          max="100" 
          value={echo}
          onChange={(e) => setEcho(Number(e.target.value))}
          disabled
        />
        <span className="value">{echo}%</span>
      </div>

      <div className="mixer-control">
        <label>Truth Level</label>
        <input 
          type="range" 
          min="0" 
          max="100" 
          value={truth}
          onChange={(e) => setTruth(Number(e.target.value))}
          disabled
        />
        <span className="value">{truth}%</span>
      </div>

      <div className="mixer-control">
        <label>Manipulation</label>
        <input 
          type="range" 
          min="0" 
          max="100" 
          value={manipulation}
          onChange={(e) => setManipulation(Number(e.target.value))}
          disabled
        />
        <span className="value">{manipulation}%</span>
      </div>

      <div className="mixer-note">
        <small>âš ï¸ Controls locked by DJ Barbara</small>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Mixer;

  return (
    
      ğŸ›ï¸ Mixer Controls

  );

### 7.2 Playlist Component

**Plik: `src/features/radio/components/Playlist.tsx`**
```tsx
import React from 'react';

interface Track {
  id: number;
  title: string;
  remix: string;
  duration: string;
  bpm: number;
  chapter: string;
}

interface PlaylistProps {
  tracks: Track[];
}

const Playlist: React.FC = ({ tracks }) => {
  return (
    
      
        #
        Track
        BPM
        Duration
        Chapter
      

      {tracks.map((track) => (
        
          {track.id}
          
            {track.title}
            {track.remix}
          
          {track.bpm}
          {track.duration}
          
            {track.chapter}
          
        
      ))}
    
  );
};

export default Playlist;
```

typescript
export interface Track {
  id: number;
  title: string;
  remix: string;
  duration: string;
  bpm: number;
  chapter: string;
}

export interface DjBarbaraData {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  aka: string;
  avatar: string;
  role: string;
  specialty: string;
  show: {
    title: string;
    schedule: string;
    description: string;
  };
  bio: string;
  stats: {
    echoLevel: number;
    truthLevel: number;
    manipulationLevel: number;
  };
  playlist: Track[];
  links: {
    story: string;
    profile: string;
  };
  featured: boolean;
  active: boolean;
}

tsx
import React from 'react';
import '../styles/mixer.css';

interface MixerProps {
  stats: {
    echoLevel: number;
    truthLevel: number;
    manipulationLevel: number;
  };
}

const Mixer: React.FC<MixerProps> = ({ stats }) => {
  return (
    <div className="dj-mixer">
      <h3>ğŸ›ï¸ Mixer Controls</h3>
      
      <div className="mixer-control">
        <label>Echo Level</label>
        <div className="mixer-slider-container">
          <input 
            type="range" 
            min="0" 
            max="100" 
            value={stats.echoLevel}
            disabled
            className="mixer-slider"
          />
          <span className="mixer-value">{stats.echoLevel}%</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="mixer-control">
        <label>Truth Level</label>
        <div className="mixer-slider-container">
          <input 
            type="range" 
            min="0" 
            max="100" 
            value={stats.truthLevel}
            disabled
            className="mixer-slider truth"
          />
          <span className="mixer-value">{stats.truthLevel}%</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="mixer-control">
        <label>Manipulation</label>
        <div className="mixer-slider-container">
          <input 
            type="range" 
            min="0" 
            max="100" 
            value={stats.manipulationLevel}
            disabled
            className="mixer-slider manipulation"
          />
          <span className="mixer-value">{stats.manipulationLevel}%</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="mixer-locked-note">
        <small>âš ï¸ Controls locked by DJ Barbara</small>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Mixer;
4.2 Komponent Playlist
UtwÃ³rz plik: src/features/dj-barbara/components/Playlist.tsx

tsx
import React from 'react';
import '../styles/playlist.css';

interface Track {
  id: number;
  title: string;
  remix: string;
  duration: string;
  bpm: number;
  chapter: string;
}

interface PlaylistProps {
  tracks: Track[];
}

const Playlist: React.FC<PlaylistProps> = ({ tracks }) => {
  return (
    <div className="dj-playlist">
      <div className="playlist-header">
        <span className="col-number">#</span>
        <span className="col-title">Track</span>
        <span className="col-bpm">BPM</span>
        <span className="col-duration">Duration</span>
        <span className="col-action">Chapter</span>
      </div>

      <div className="playlist-tracks">
        {tracks.map((track) => (
          <div key={track.id} className="playlist-track">
            <span className="col-number">{track.id}</span>
            <div className="col-title">
              <div className="track-title">{track.title}</div>
              <div className="track-remix">{track.remix}</div>
            </div>
            <span className="col-bpm">{track.bpm}</span>
            <span className="col-duration">{track.duration}</span>
            <a 
              href={`/polana-klamstw/${track.chapter}`}
              className="col-action button-link"
            >
              Czytaj â†’
            </a>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Playlist;

10. OPCJONALNE ULEPSZENIA
10.1 Easter Egg - Secret Click
W komponencie Radio dodaj ukryty element, ktÃ³ry po 7 klikniÄ™ciach przekierowuje do DJ Barbara:

  const newCount = secretClicks + 1;
  setSecretClicks(newCount);
  
  if (newCount === 7) {
    window.location.href = '/dj-barbara';
  }
};

// W JSX:

  style={{ 
    cursor: 'pointer', 
    opacity: 0.05,
    position: 'absolute',
    bottom: 20,
    right: 20
  }}

  ğŸ§
</div>
